  /*
    This is kind of gross but let me explain.
    The triangle-down icon in the user lists menu component needs to be larger on small screens
    but Primer doesn't accept a responsive value for size.
    So instead we use CSS to override the size on small screens only, to match the ⭐ button beside it.
    The selector is written this way to avoid affecting other buttons inside the lists dropdown.
  */
  @media (max-width: 767px) {
    .icon-button-group .BtnGroup-parent > * > button:first-child {
      height: var(--control-medium-size);
      width: var(--control-medium-size);
      min-width: var(--control-medium-size);
    }
  }

  /* No idea what this is though. It was like this when I got here. */
  @media (min-width: 544px) {
    .icon-button-group .SelectMenu {
      right: auto !important;
      left: 0 !important;
    }
  }

\u003ccode\u003essort\u003c/code\u003e needs to make changes to a \u003ca href=\"https://black.readthedocs.io/en/stable/\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003eblack\u003c/a\u003e conformant file, the result will \u003ccode\u003essort\u003c/code\u003e conformant.\nWe recommend that you reformat using \u003ca href=\"https://pycqa.github.io/isort/\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003eisort\u003c/a\u003e and \u003ca 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003essort\u003c/code\u003e will sort top level statements and statements in class bodies.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eWhen sorting top level statements, \u003ccode\u003essort\u003c/code\u003e follows three simple rules:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eStatements must always be moved after the statements that they depend on, unless there is a cycle.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eIf there is a cycle, the order of statements within the cycle must not be changed.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eIf there is no dependency between statements then, to the greatest extent possible, the original order should be kept.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThese rules result in low level building blocks being moved to the top of modules, with higher level logic going at the bottom.\nThe \u003ca href=\"#why-does-ssort-sort-bottom-up-rather-than-top-down\"\u003eFAQ\u003c/a\u003e goes into some detail about why this order was chosen.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe rules for sorting class bodies are more complicated.\nClass methods are generally only called from outside the class and so there aren't usually many interdependencies from which to derive structure.\n\u003ccode\u003essort\u003c/code\u003e therefore ignores (deferred) dependencies between d`under and public methods and instead divides up class statements into hard-coded groups that it arranges in the following order:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eThe class docstring.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSpecial attributes, i.e. \u003ccode\u003e__slots__\u003c/code\u003e or \u003ccode\u003e__doc__\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eInner classes.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eRegular attributes.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eLifecycle d'under methods, e.g. \u003ccode\u003e__init__\u003c/code\u003e or \u003ccode\u003e__new__\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ePublic methods, and unused private methods.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eOther d'under methods, e.g. \u003ccode\u003e__getattr__\u003c/code\u003e or \u003ccode\u003e__len__\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eApart from the docstring, this order is essentially arbitrary.\nIt is was chosen as being representative of current standard industry practice.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eD'under methods are arranged in a hard coded order within their group.\nStatements in other groups are left in their original order.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003ePrivate methods should only be called from other methods in the class, and so are mixed in topologically.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eIf a class-definition-time dependency is detected between two statements preserving the relative order of the linked statements will take priority.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ca name=\"user-content-frequently-asked-questions\"\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eWhy does \u003ccode\u003essort\u003c/code\u003e sort bottom-up rather than 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003ePython is a scripting language, which means that the body of each module is evaluated, statement by statement, from top to bottom.\nIn almost all cases, things must be defined before they can be used.\nAttempting, in the subset of cases where it is possible, to reverse the order is difficult to do safely and leads to inconsistency with the cases where top-down ordering is impossible.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ca name=\"user-content-top-down-ordering-is-only-possible-when-lookups-are-deferred\"\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch4 tabindex=\"-1\" evaluated yet.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eAs far as I am aware, there is only one way to reference a variable that has not been bound yet, and that is to close over it in a function dir=\"auto\"\u003eTop-down ordering makes code navigation difficult\u003c/h4\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-top-down-ordering-makes-code-navigation-difficult\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Top-down ordering makes code navigation difficult\" href=\"#top-down-ordering-makes-code-navigation-difficult\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eWith bottom-up ordering, navigation is easy.\nIf you want to find where a variable is defined you scroll up.\nIf you want to find where a variable is used you scroll down.\nThese rules are reliable, and straightforward for programmers to learn and apply.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eWith top-down order, navigation is more tricky.\nIf you want to find where a variable is defined you scroll down, unless the variable is a constant or an import, or the variable is referenced here at import time, or the variable is referenced somewhere else at import time, or any of the many other special cases.\nIf you want to find where a variable is used, you basically have to scan the whole file.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eEvery special case added to the sorting tool is a special case that programmers need to learn if they are to navigate quickly, and top-down ordering requires a lot of special cases.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ca name=\"user-content-why-doesn-t-ssort-allow-me-to-configure-x\"\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" itemprop="text"><div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">SSort</h1><a id="user-content-ssort" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: SSort" <p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/bwhmather/ssort/actions/workflows/ci.yaml"><img alt="Build Status" src="https://github.com/bwhmather/ssort/actions/workflows/ci.yaml/badge.svg?branch=master" style="max-width: 100%;"></a> <a href="https://coveralls.io/github/bwhmather/ssort?branch=master" rel="nofollow"><img alt="Cocerage" src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/4e9584d7b1a78028d94d6d47dbda322feb3a8faccbd573b6a14d68476cd9e155/68747470733a2f2f636f766572616c6c732e696f2f7265706f732f6769746875622f6277686d61746865722f73736f72742f62616467652e7376673f6272616e63683d6d6173746572" data-canonical-src="https://coveralls.io/repos/github/bwhmather/ssort/badge.svg?branch=master" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">The python source code sorter.</p>
<p dir="auto">Sorts the contents of python modules so that statements are placed after the things they depend on, but leaves grouping to the programmer.
Groups class members by type and enforces topological sorting of methods.</p>
<p dir="auto">Makes old fashioned code navigation easier, you can always scroll up to see where something is defined, and reduces bikeshedding.</p>
<p dir="auto">Compatible with and intended to complement <a href="https://pycqa.github.io/isort/" rel="nofollow">isort</a> and <a href="https://black.readthedocs.io/en/stable/" rel="nofollow">black</a>.</p>
<p dir="auto">Before:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto"><pre><span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">module</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">BaseClass</span>

<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">function</span>():
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-en">_dependency</span>()

<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">_decorator</span>(<span class="pl-s1">fn</span>):
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">fn</span>

<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">_decorator</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">_dependency</span>():
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-en">Class</span>()

    <span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">public_method</span>(<span class="pl-s1">self</span>):
        <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">self</span>

    <span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">__init__</span>(<span class="pl-s1">self</span>):
        <span class="pl-k">pass</span></pre><div class="zeroclipboard-container">

def function():
    return _dependency()

def _decorator(fn):
    return fn

@_decorator
def _dependency():
    return Class()

class Class(BaseClass):
    def public_method(self):

<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto"><pre><span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">module</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">BaseClass</span>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Installation</h2><a id="user-content-installation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Installation" href="#installation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">SSort can be installed manually using pip.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto"><pre>$ pip install ssort</pre><div class="zeroclipboard-container">

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Usage</h2><a id="user-content-usage" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Usage" href="#usage"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">To check that a file is correctly sorted use the --check flag.
--diff can be passed to see what changes <code>ssort</code> would make.</p>

<p dir="auto">To allow <code>ssort</code> to rearrange your file, simply invoke with no extra flags.
If <code>ssort</code> needs to make changes to a <a href="https://black.readthedocs.io/en/stable/" rel="nofollow">black</a> conformant file, the result will not necessarily be <a href="https://black.readthedocs.io/en/stable/" rel="nofollow">black</a> conformant.
The result of running <a href="https://black.readthedocs.io/en/stable/" rel="nofollow">black</a> on an <code>ssort</code> conformant file will always be <code>ssort</code> conformant.
We recommend that you reformat using <a href="https://pycqa.github.io/isort/" rel="nofollow">isort</a> and <a href="https://black.readthedocs.io/en/stable/" rel="nofollow">black</a> immediately after running <code>ssort</code>.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto"><pre>$ ssort src/ tests/<span class="pl-k">;</span> isort src/ tests/<span class="pl-k">;</span> black src/ tests/</pre><div class="zeroclipboard-container">

and registering ssort in your .pre-commit-config.yaml.</p>

<a name="user-content-output"></a>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Output</h2><a id="user-content-output" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Output" href="#output"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><code>ssort</code> will sort top level statements and statements in class bodies.</p>
<p dir="auto">When sorting top level statements, <code>ssort</code> follows three simple rules:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Statements must always be moved after the statements that they depend on, unless there is a cycle.</li>
<li>If there is a cycle, the order of statements within the cycle must not be changed.</li>
<li>If there is no dependency between statements then, to the greatest extent possible, the original order should be kept.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">These rules result in low level building blocks being moved to the top of modules, with higher level logic going at the bottom.
The <a href="#why-does-ssort-sort-bottom-up-rather-than-top-down">FAQ</a> goes into some detail about why this order was chosen.</p>
<p dir="auto">The rules for sorting class bodies are more complicated.
Class methods are generally only called from outside the class and so there aren't usually many interdependencies from which to derive structure.
<code>ssort</code> therefore ignores (deferred) dependencies between d`under and public methods and instead divides up class statements into hard-coded groups that it arranges in the following order:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The class docstring.</li>
<li>Special attributes, i.e. <code>__slots__</code> or <code>__doc__</code>.</li>
<li>Inner classes.</li>
<li>Regular attributes.</li>
<li>Lifecycle d'under methods, e.g. <code>__init__</code> or <code>__new__</code>.</li>
<li>Public methods, and unused private methods.</li>
<li>Other d'under methods, e.g. <code>__getattr__</code> or <code>__len__</code>.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Apart from the docstring, this order is essentially arbitrary.
It is was chosen as being representative of current standard industry practice.</p>
<p dir="auto">D'under methods are arranged in a hard coded order within their group.
Statements in other groups are left in their original order.</p>
<p dir="auto">Private methods should only be called from other methods in the class, and so are mixed in topologically.</p>
<p dir="auto">If a class-definition-time dependency is detected between two statements preserving the relative order of the linked statements will take priority.</p>
<a name="user-content-frequently-asked-questions"></a>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Frequently Asked Questions</h2><a id="user-content-frequently-asked-questions" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Frequently Asked Questions" href="#frequently-asked-questions"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<a name="user-content-why-does-ssort-sort-bottom-up-rather-than-top-down"></a>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Why does <code>ssort</code> sort bottom-up rather than top-down?</h3><a id="user-content-why-does-ssort-sort-bottom-up-rather-than-top-down" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Why does ssort sort bottom-up rather than top-down?" href="#why-does-ssort-sort-bottom-up-rather-than-top-down"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Python is a scripting language, which means that the body of each module is evaluated, statement by statement, from top to bottom.
In almost all cases, things must be defined before they can be used.
Attempting, in the subset of cases where it is possible, to reverse the order is difficult to do safely and leads to inconsistency with the cases where top-down ordering is impossible.</p>
<a name="user-content-top-down-ordering-is-only-possible-when-lookups-are-deferred"></a>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Top-down ordering is only possible when lookups are deferred</h4><a id="user-content-top-down-ordering-is-only-possible-when-lookups-are-deferred" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Top-down ordering is only possible when lookups are deferred" href="#top-down-ordering-is-only-possible-when-lookups-are-deferred"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Top-down ordering is only possible when lookups are deferred, but in most cases, lookups happen immediately.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto"><pre><span class="pl-c"># Broken.</span>

<span class="pl-s1">variable</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">dependency</span>()

<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">dependency</span>():
    ...</pre><div class="zeroclipboard-container">
    <clipboard-copy aria-label="Copy" class="ClipboardButton btn btn-invisible js-clipboard-copy m-2 p-0 d-flex flex-justify-center flex-items-center" data-copy-feedback="Copied!" data-tooltip-direction="w" value="# Broken.

variable = dependency()

def dependency():
    ..." tabindex="0" role="button">
      <svg aria-hidden="true" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" data-view-component="true" class="octicon octicon-copy js-clipboard-copy-icon">
    <path d="M0 6.75C0 5.784.784 5 1.75 5h1.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-1.5a.25.25 0 0 0-.25.25v7.5c0 .138.112.25.25.25h7.5a.25.25 0 0 0 .25-.25v-1.5a.75.75 0 0 1 1.5 0v1.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 9.25 16h-7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 0 14.25Z"></path><path d="M5 1.75C5 .784 5.784 0 6.75 0h7.5C15.216 0 16 .784 16 1.75v7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 14.25 11h-7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 5 9.25Zm1.75-.25a.25.25 0 0 0-.25.25v7.5c0 .138.112.25.25.25h7.5a.25.25 0 0 0 .25-.25v-7.5a.25.25 0 0 0-.25-.25Z"></path>
</svg>
      <svg aria-hidden="true" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" data-view-component="true" class="octicon octicon-check js-clipboard-check-icon color-fg-success d-none">
    <path d="M13.78 4.22a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.06l-7.25 7.25a.75.75 0 0 1-1.06 0L2.22 9.28a.751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018L6 10.94l6.72-6.72a.75.75 0 0 1 1.06 0Z"></path>
</svg>
    </clipboard-copy>
  </div></div>
<p dir="auto">In this example python will try to find <code>dependency</code> in the <code>locals()</code> dict when the first line is evaluated, and fail because the statement that defines it has not been evaluated yet.</p>
<p dir="auto">As far as I am aware, there is only one way to reference a variable that has not been bound yet, and that is to close over it in a function definition.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto"><pre><span class="pl-c"># Working.</span>

<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">function</span>():
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-en">dependency</span>()

<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">dependency</span>():
    ...</pre><div class="zeroclipboard-container">
    <clipboard-copy aria-label="Copy" class="ClipboardButton btn btn-invisible js-clipboard-copy m-2 p-0 d-flex flex-justify-center flex-items-center" data-copy-feedback="Copied!" data-tooltip-direction="w" value="# Working.

def function():
    return dependency()

def dependency():
    ..." tabindex="0" role="button">
      <svg aria-hidden="true" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" data-view-component="true" class="octicon octicon-copy js-clipboard-copy-icon">
    <path d="M0 6.75C0 5.784.784 5 1.75 5h1.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-1.5a.25.25 0 0 0-.25.25v7.5c0 .138.112.25.25.25h7.5a.25.25 0 0 0 .25-.25v-1.5a.75.75 0 0 1 1.5 0v1.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 9.25 16h-7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 0 14.25Z"></path><path d="M5 1.75C5 .784 5.784 0 6.75 0h7.5C15.216 0 16 .784 16 1.75v7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 14.25 11h-7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 5 9.25Zm1.75-.25a.25.25 0 0 0-.25.25v7.5c0 .138.112.25.25.25h7.5a.25.25 0 0 0 .25-.25v-7.5a.25.25 0 0 0-.25-.25Z"></path>
</svg>
      <svg aria-hidden="true" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" data-view-component="true" class="octicon octicon-check js-clipboard-check-icon color-fg-success d-none">
    <path d="M13.78 4.22a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.06l-7.25 7.25a.75.75 0 0 1-1.06 0L2.22 9.28a.751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018L6 10.94l6.72-6.72a.75.75 0 0 1 1.06 0Z"></path>
</svg>
    </clipboard-copy>
  </div></div>
<p dir="auto">This is because the lookup is deferred until after <code>function</code> is called, which in this case doesn't happen until both functions are defined.</p>
<a name="user-content-top-down-ordering-fails-unsafe"></a>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Top-down ordering fails unsafe</h4><a id="user-content-top-down-ordering-fails-unsafe" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Top-down ordering fails unsafe" href="#top-down-ordering-fails-unsafe"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">In cases where lookups are deferred, they may not be deferred sufficiently far to allow the dependant statement to be sorted before its dependencies.</p>
<p dir="auto">Take the following example formatted in bottom-up order.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto"><pre><span class="pl-c"># Hidden runtime dependency example sorted bottom-up.</span>

<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">_shared_dep</span>():
    ...

<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">_decorator</span>(<span class="pl-s1">fn</span>):
    <span class="pl-en">_shared_dep</span>()
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">fn</span>

<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">_decorator</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">top_level</span>():
    <span class="pl-en">_shared_dep</span>()</pre><div class="zeroclipboard-container">
    <clipboard-copy aria-label="Copy" class="ClipboardButton btn btn-invisible js-clipboard-copy m-2 p-0 d-flex flex-justify-center flex-items-center" data-copy-feedback="Copied!" data-tooltip-direction="w" value="# Hidden runtime dependency example sorted bottom-up.

def _shared_dep():
    ...

def _decorator(fn):
    _shared_dep()
    return fn

@_decorator
def top_level():
    _shared_dep()" tabindex="0" role="button">
      <svg aria-hidden="true" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" data-view-component="true" class="octicon octicon-copy js-clipboard-copy-icon">
    <path d="M0 6.75C0 5.784.784 5 1.75 5h1.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-1.5a.25.25 0 0 0-.25.25v7.5c0 .138.112.25.25.25h7.5a.25.25 0 0 0 .25-.25v-1.5a.75.75 0 0 1 1.5 0v1.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 9.25 16h-7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 0 14.25Z"></path><path d="M5 1.75C5 .784 5.784 0 6.75 0h7.5C15.216 0 16 .784 16 1.75v7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 14.25 11h-7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 5 9.25Zm1.75-.25a.25.25 0 0 0-.25.25v7.5c0 .138.112.25.25.25h7.5a.25.25 0 0 0 .25-.25v-7.5a.25.25 0 0 0-.25-.25Z"></path>
</svg>
      <svg aria-hidden="true" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" data-view-component="true" class="octicon octicon-check js-clipboard-check-icon color-fg-success d-none">
    <path d="M13.78 4.22a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.06l-7.25 7.25a.75.75 0 0 1-1.06 0L2.22 9.28a.751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018L6 10.94l6.72-6.72a.75.75 0 0 1 1.06 0Z"></path>
</svg>
    </clipboard-copy>
  </div></div>
<p dir="auto">A naive analysis would suggest that <code>_shared_dep</code> is a runtime dependency and can safely be moved to the bottom of the script.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto"><pre><span class="pl-c"># Hidden runtime dependency example sorted top-down using naive analysis.</span>

<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">_decorator</span>(<span class="pl-s1">fn</span>):
    <span class="pl-en">_shared_dep</span>()
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">fn</span>

<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">_decorator</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">top_level</span>():
    <span class="pl-en">_shared_dep</span>()

<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">_shared_dep</span>():
    ...</pre><div class="zeroclipboard-container">
    <clipboard-copy aria-label="Copy" class="ClipboardButton btn btn-invisible js-clipboard-copy m-2 p-0 d-flex flex-justify-center flex-items-center" data-copy-feedback="Copied!" data-tooltip-direction="w" value="# Hidden runtime dependency example sorted top-down using naive analysis.

def _decorator(fn):
    _shared_dep()
    return fn

@_decorator
def top_level():
    _shared_dep()

def _shared_dep():
    ..." tabindex="0" role="button">
      <svg aria-hidden="true" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" data-view-component="true" class="octicon octicon-copy js-clipboard-copy-icon">
    <path d="M0 6.75C0 5.784.784 5 1.75 5h1.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-1.5a.25.25 0 0 0-.25.25v7.5c0 .138.112.25.25.25h7.5a.25.25 0 0 0 .25-.25v-1.5a.75.75 0 0 1 1.5 0v1.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 9.25 16h-7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 0 14.25Z"></path><path d="M5 1.75C5 .784 5.784 0 6.75 0h7.5C15.216 0 16 .784 16 1.75v7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 14.25 11h-7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 5 9.25Zm1.75-.25a.25.25 0 0 0-.25.25v7.5c0 .138.112.25.25.25h7.5a.25.25 0 0 0 .25-.25v-7.5a.25.25 0 0 0-.25-.25Z"></path>
</svg>
      <svg aria-hidden="true" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" data-view-component="true" class="octicon octicon-check js-clipboard-check-icon color-fg-success d-none">
    <path d="M13.78 4.22a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.06l-7.25 7.25a.75.75 0 0 1-1.06 0L2.22 9.28a.751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018L6 10.94l6.72-6.72a.75.75 0 0 1 1.06 0Z"></path>
</svg>

  </div></div>
<p dir="auto">This will result in a <code>NameError</code> as <code>_shared_dep</code> will not have been bound when <code>_decorator</code> is invoked.</p>
<p dir="auto">More powerful static analysls can mitigate this problem, but any missed hard references are likely to result in the program being broken.
Bottom-up sorting can only force broken reorderings when static analysis misses a reference that results in a cycle.</p>
<a name="user-content-top-down-ordering-needs-special-cases-for-constants-and-imports"></a>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Top-down ordering needs special cases for constants and imports</h4><a id="user-content-top-down-ordering-needs-special-cases-for-constants-and-imports" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Top-down ordering needs special cases for constants and imports" href="#top-down-ordering-needs-special-cases-for-constants-and-imports"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Even the most die hard proponent of top down ordering would not argue that <code>import</code> statements should be moved to the bottom of the file.</p>
<p dir="auto">Take the following example:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto"><pre><span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">module</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">first_dep</span>

<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">second_dep</span>():
    ...

<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">decorator</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">function</span>():
    <span class="pl-en">first_dep</span>()
    <span class="pl-en">second_dep</span>()</pre><div class="zeroclipboard-container">
    <clipboard-copy aria-label="Copy" class="ClipboardButton btn btn-invisible js-clipboard-copy m-2 p-0 d-flex flex-justify-center flex-items-center" data-copy-feedback="Copied!" data-tooltip-direction="w" value="from module import first_dep

def second_dep():
    ...

@decorator
def function():
    first_dep()
    second_dep()" tabindex="0" role="button">
      <svg aria-hidden="true" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" data-view-component="true" class="octicon octicon-copy js-clipboard-copy-icon">
    <path d="M0 6.75C0 5.784.784 5 1.75 5h1.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-1.5a.25.25 0 0 0-.25.25v7.5c0 .138.112.25.25.25h7.5a.25.25 0 0 0 .25-.25v-1.5a.75.75 0 0 1 1.5 0v1.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 9.25 16h-7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 0 14.25Z"></path><path d="M5 1.75C5 .784 5.784 0 6.75 0h7.5C15.216 0 16 .784 16 1.75v7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 14.25 11h-7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 5 9.25Zm1.75-.25a.25.25 0 0 0-.25.25v7.5c0 .138.112.25.25.25h7.5a.25.25 0 0 0 .25-.25v-7.5a.25.25 0 0 0-.25-.25Z"></path>
</svg>
      <svg aria-hidden="true" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" data-view-component="true" class="octicon octicon-check js-clipboard-check-icon color-fg-success d-none">
    <path d="M13.78 4.22a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.06l-7.25 7.25a.75.75 0 0 1-1.06 0L2.22 9.28a.751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018L6 10.94l6.72-6.72a.75.75 0 0 1 1.06 0Z"></path>

  </div></div>
<p dir="auto">A strict top-down sort would see it reordered with the <code>first_dep</code> import at the bottom of the file.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto"><pre><span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">other_module</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">decorator</span>

<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">decorator</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">function</span>():
    <span class="pl-en">first_dep</span>()
    <span class="pl-en">second_dep</span>()

<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">second_dep</span>():
    ...

<span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">module</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">first_dep</span></pre><div class="zeroclipboard-container">
    <clipboard-copy aria-label="Copy" class="ClipboardButton btn btn-invisible js-clipboard-copy m-2 p-0 d-flex flex-justify-center flex-items-center" data-copy-feedback="Copied!" data-tooltip-direction="w" value="from other_module import decorator

def function():
    first_dep()
    second_dep()

def second_dep():
    ...

      <svg aria-hidden="true" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" data-view-component="true" class="octicon octicon-copy js-clipboard-copy-icon">
    <path d="M0 6.75C0 5.784.784 5 1.75 5h1.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-1.5a.25.25 0 0 0-.25.25v7.5c0 .138.112.25.25.25h7.5a.25.25 0 0 0 .25-.25v-1.5a.75.75 0 0 1 1.5 0v1.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 9.25 16h-7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 0 14.25Z"></path><path d="M5 1.75C5 .784 5.784 0 6.75 0h7.5C15.216 0 16 .784 16 1.75v7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 14.25 11h-7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 5 9.25Zm1.75-.25a.25.25 0 0 0-.25.25v7.5c0 .138.112.25.25.25h7.5a.25.25 0 0 0 .25-.25v-7.5a.25.25 0 0 0-.25-.25Z"></path>

    <path d="M13.78 4.22a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.06l-7.25 7.25a.75.75 0 0 1-1.06 0L2.22 9.28a.751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018L6 10.94l6.72-6.72a.75.75 0 0 1 1.06 0Z"></path>

<a name="user-content-top-down-ordering-makes-code-navigation-difficult"></a>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Top-down ordering makes code navigation difficult</h4><a id="user-content-top-down-ordering-makes-code-navigation-difficult" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Top-down ordering makes code navigation difficult" href="#top-down-ordering-makes-code-navigation-difficult"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">With bottom-up ordering, navigation is easy.
If you want to find where a variable is defined you scroll up.
If you want to find where a variable is used you scroll down.
These rules are reliable, and straightforward for programmers to learn and apply.</p>
<p dir="auto">With top-down order, navigation is more tricky.
If you want to find where a variable is defined you scroll down, unless the variable is a constant or an import, or the variable is referenced here at import time, or the variable is referenced somewhere else at import time, or any of the many other special cases.
If you want to find where a variable is used, you basically have to scan the whole file.</p>
<p dir="auto">Every special case added to the sorting tool is a special case that programmers need to learn if they are to navigate quickly, and top-down ordering requires a lot of special cases.</p>
<a name="user-content-why-doesn-t-ssort-allow-me-to-configure-x"></a>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Why doesn't ssort allow me to configure X?</h3><a id="user-content-why-doesnt-ssort-allow-me-to-configure-x" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Why doesn't ssort allow me to configure X?" href="#why-doesnt-ssort-allow-me-to-configure-x"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><code>ssort</code> aims to bring about ecosystem wide consistency in how python source files are organised.
If this can be achieved then it will help all programmers familiar with its conventions to navigate unfamiliar codebases, and it will reduce arguments between programmers who prefer different conventions.
This only works if those conventions can't be changed.</p>
<a name="user-content-why-was-ssort-created"></a>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Why was ssort created?</h3><a id="user-content-why-was-ssort-created" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Why was ssort created?" href="#why-was-ssort-created"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><code>ssort</code> exists because its author was too lazy to implement jump-to-definition in his text editor, and decided that it would be easier to just reformat all of the world's python code to make it possible to navigate by scrolling.</p>
<a name="user-content-links"></a>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Links</h2><a id="user-content-links" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Links" href="#links"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
